< text>
So we were super excited to go to this beautiful place for Valentines Day. I made reservations a week before for 8:30pm. It was a $200 deposit to make the reservations and applies to your dinner. We got there and waited in line about 15 min to check in. Finally got to the front and we were told we had to wait another 45 min for our table to be ready either at the bar or stand around and wait. Mind you, there is another line for the bar which looks to be about another 30 min wait, and it's cold outside because it's only outdoor dining because of covid. 1 hour later I go back to the front to check on the table, they say it's going to be another 30 to 45 min wait. It's already 9:30pm so we wouldn't be getting a table til almost 10:30. We canceled the table and went to Denny's lol smh. They told me that they overbooked and it really got away from them somehow. They said people were only allowed to be at their table for about 75 min and staying longer, but they weren't doing anything to keep ppl within their time. So overall, I was highly disappointed with how things went for Valentines Day. The food was probably really good but I would know because it took way too long. I've never had a reservation at a restaurant and had to wait more than 15 min, if that. I would probably go on a regular day just to try the food but never again on a holiday.

*UPDATE*

Here's an update after what happened on Valentine's Day. I was contacted to allow them to accommodate me and my partner for another dinner at the date of my choice. We did set a date and went back for the on the house dinner and drinks and let me tell you, it was exactly what I thought it would be. The food was amazing, the drinks were great, and the customer service was outstanding. The manager even came over to check on us and apologized for the Valentine's Day dinner fiasco. He admitted that it was definitely a crazy night and I see that they did improve on how to handle those kinds of occasions better. The music and atmosphere was also great. The waiter, Niko, was amazing and very attentive and accommodating. They even brought us a surprise dessert that was delicious! Overall, I truly appreciate them making up for the last visit and would definitely go back for dinner and drinks. STK has become a favorite and can't wait to try other items on their menu. Definitely give them a try.< /text>

< text>
During the pandemic this location is currently only seating people outdoors. It can get a bit cold and breezy so bring a jacket, especially if you're having cold drinks! Make sure you check when their happy hour is! I went on a saturday and it went from 3 pm to 6:30 pm. They have half priced cocktails($9.50) and half priced oysters! ($2) the oysters were absolutely delicious.  We were told that the king crab oscar was a must have so my entire party ordered it, but I honestly wouldn't again. The crab pieces were all broken up and small, and there were tons of shell pieces inside. The location has valet parking, and some parking on nearby streets, but some streets require a permit so double check the signs! It may conjure up stuffy, traditional, manly, but STK manages to have the fine dining in a space where you can socialize and party without holding back. Tiffany Duong<//user_name>
< Date>
1413230087960< /Date>
<rating>4</rating><text>Life is good when you can afford to come to a shi-shi fancy hollywood steakhouse like STK on a whim with some good friends, enjoy some choice cuts of meat on sizzling plates, and down it with some vino and chatter while admiring the pretty people coming in.

DineLA was happening, so some college buddies and I made a date for me to try out  STK. One of my steak-and-bacon buddies had been rating this place #2 steakhouse in LA, and I had to try it. In the end, I had to agree with him. #2 steak in LA.

THE SCENE
Walked in, and was immediately impressed by the entry. Long awning with waterfalls and stone walls leads you in on a red carpet. Yes, we sure are hollywood adjacent. The hostesses are all in black, all young and pretty, and they lead you to your table once everyone is there. The tables are in a big open area, so it definitely isn't like an old-school mobster-esque steakhouse with enclosed booths and dark decor. Here it was dark, but only enough to be chic. The walls were textured and well lit. It felt slightly too masculine for a romantic date, but then again it still was a steakhouse. It was perfect for a friend reunion.

THE MUSIC
Normally, i would never dedicate an entire review section to the music, but holy balls whatever the DJ there was spinning had be in the best mood ever. Mashups -- EDM with 80s classic ballads, old school rock and kid cudi, I mean the most crazy stuff, but it was SO GOOD. I kept asking my human-jukebox friend what each song was because I could not stop listening and talking about how great the music was. Definitely will be back for Happy Hour to enjoy the tunes, wine, and cheap bites!

THE FOOD
After seeing some mixed reviews, I was worried I might not like my steak. After all, steak and I go way back, and I've been spoiled to have eaten some fabulous steaks in my day. I'm personally a char and sizzling plate kinda gal, which makes me partial to a certain Beverly Hills M****** Steakhouse that just makes it perfection. The steaks at STK were very decent indeed. The taste was spot on -- not too light a flavoring. I had the filet mignon (not bone-in) and it was still very delicious. The cut was soft to the knife, and slightly warm inside. The plate didn't overcook the meat at all. I also tried the skirt steak and the bone-in ribeye. The ribeye was pretty good, but I am a filet girl. The char was not as strong as I would have liked it, but I will take a good flavoring over an over-char. This was a well-cooked and very tasty slab of cow.

The parmesan truffle fries are rectangular 2x4 esque cuts of potato perfectly fried. steamy on the inside and crunchy outside, with parmesan that gave a perfect flavor and just enough truffle oil to me amazing.

The corn pudding was sweet but good. Very smooth. I thought it was mashed potatoes when I first had it.

The vanilla panna cotta was pretty well executed as well -- very soft, and served with nicely complimenting flavors.

OVERALL
I loved my night here. The food was not the best, but it was pretty damn good. Memorable and very nice night out on the town in Hollywood. I wouldn't hesitate to come back and enjoy another meal here.

OTHER TIPS
Go during happy hour if the price tag is keeping you away
Try to find street parking (a little difficult) or bring $9 for valet
Dress code is striclty enforced - no flip flops or beach wear
Go during dineLA -- 3 courses (steak included) for $45 and $14 for 2 drinks add-ons. GREAT DEAL.</text>< pictures>

My recommendation is to avoid this place like the plague unless you are the police or tax fraud investigator.

Follow up to owner's comments:

Isn't it interesting how everyone who posts a critical review of this business is a pessimistic, manipulative, evil person who for some reason just wants to pick on poor Eli?  Maybe that's why there are so many negative posts.  He spends his time trying to discredit these honest, accurate reviews rather than doing something about the legitimate complaints.

We did not make our purchase from a home show, we visited the showroom on McKinley.  And at no time was my wife there without me.  I do not even know why he felt this info was relevant to his argument, but it is a complete lie.

< text>
According to the name, this grocery store hidden in the corner of Pioneer blvd and South Street in predominantly Asian Indian Artesia has become the place for shopping among Sri Lankansâ€™ and South Indians. The store carries freshly imported Sri Lankan fish and the best quality Sri Lankan canned food. To add during weekends they cater freshly made short eats, lunch packets, milk toffees, kottu Rotti, lamprais and many more Sri Lankan dishes. The lamprais, the hybrid version of the Dutch is a major seller at this place. Only limited number is available over the weekend. <user_name>Spanish Fly< /user_name><date>1476931166472</date><rating>3< /rating>< Review>
this is no longer Beacon. It has been a  Valero gas station (1 of 2 Valero's in this town) for some time.  There are 2 Valero gas stations in this small town, both are on the same street.  Whether you are entering or leaving  the town from one of only  two exits, you will see a Valero gas station.  This Valero gas station is across the street from McDonald's and next door to Carl's Jr.  The gentlemen that run this gas station are very sweet and attentive. They are very polite and keep the gas station bathrooms very clean and the shop is always well stocked. This Valero gas station also offers propane services. If you need a propane refill you can get it here at a reasonable price. However , don't come here if you need air for your tires because the machine has been out of service for some time (part of the reason why I'm giving it only a 3 STAR rating).< /Review>

< text>
Beautifully maintained cemetery in palo alto. Some of the plots are out in the open, others are in more shaded areas under large trees. Walking around the grounds you get a hint of peoples stories, their history and the history of the country. Its strangely beautiful to see so many generations together, like time progresses there more slowly and 10 generations interact instead of just 3.</text>
